## Analysis

The Ground Truth (GT) numerical expression is:
$$-0.17496 \cdot A^2 + 0.59132 \cdot \sin(\log(A + 1))$$

Let me check the candidates systematically.

**Candidate 24**: `A**2*c0 + c1 + c2*sin(c3*log(A*c4 + 1) + c5)`

Setting:
- c0 = -0.17496 (to match the A² term)
- c1 = 0 (no constant offset in GT)
- c2 = 0.59132 (amplitude of sin)
- c3 = 1 (coefficient of log)
- c4 = 1 (so A*c4 + 1 = A + 1)
- c5 = 0 (no phase shift)

This gives: $-0.17496 \cdot A^2 + 0 + 0.59132 \cdot \sin(1 \cdot \log(A \cdot 1 + 1) + 0) = -0.17496 \cdot A^2 + 0.59132 \cdot \sin(\log(A+1))$

This **exactly matches** the GT.

**Candidate 44**: `A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6)`

**Candidate 48**: `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6)`

Setting c1=0 and the rest as above also works.

**Candidate 73**: `A**2*c0 + c1 + c2*exp(c3/(A + c4)) + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8)`

Setting c2=0 (eliminating exp term) and appropriate other constants also works.

**Candidate 61**: `A*c0/(A + c1) + A**c2*c3 + c4 + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8)`

Setting c0=0, c2=2, c3=-0.17496, c4=0, c5=0.59132, c6=1, c7=1, c8=0 works.

Multiple candidates match, with **Candidate 24** being the most direct and clean match.

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK10)

GT: -c0*A**c1 + c2*_t*sin(log(A + c3))
Candidates evaluated: 109
Matched candidate IDs: [21, 24, 44, 48, 61, 73]
Matched candidates: ["A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(A**2*c4) + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8)", "A**2*c0 + c1 + c2*sin(c3*log(A*c4 + 1) + c5)", "A**c0*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6)", "A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6)", "A*c0/(A + c1) + A**c2*c3 + c4 + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8)", "A**2*c0 + c1 + c2*exp(c3/(A + c4)) + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8)"]

I need to determine which candidates can be made equivalent to the Ground Truth:

**GT: -0.17495597*A² + 0.59132419*sin(log(A + 1))**

This is a sum of two terms: a quadratic in A and a sin(log(A+1)) term.

Let me analyze each candidate systematically. I need to check if each candidate's functional form can reduce to `c*A² + d*sin(log(A+1))` for some constants.

Key basis functions in GT:
1. **A²** (polynomial)
2. **sin(log(A+1))** (transcendental)

No dependence on t (the _t in GT is absorbed into the constant c2*_t = 0.59132419).

Let me go through candidates, focusing on structural compatibility:

**Candidates with sin(log(...)) terms:**

**Candidate 3:** `c0 + c1*sin(A*c2 + c3) + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6 + 1) + c7)`
Has sin(log(A+1)) but no A² term. Has sin(A) instead. sin(A) ≠ A². **NO MATCH**

**Candidate 21:** `A²*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(A²*c4) + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7 + 1) + c8)`
Set c1=0, c4=0 (making exp term = c3), absorb constants. Becomes: A²*c0 + (c2+c3) + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7+1) + c8). Set c6=1, c7=1, c8=0. This gives A²*c0 + const + c5*sin(log(A+1)). But GT has no constant term. Set c2+c3=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 24:** `A²*c0 + c1 + c2*sin(c3*log(A*c4 + 1) + c5)`
Set c1=0, c3=1, c4=1, c5=0. Gives A²*c0 + c2*sin(log(A+1)). **MATCH**

**Candidate 44:** `A^c0*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6)`
Set c0=2, c4=1, c5=1, c6=0, c2=0. Gives c1*A² + c3*sin(log(A+1)). **MATCH**

**Candidate 48:** `A²*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*sin(c4*log(A*c5 + 1) + c6)`
Set c1=0, c2=0, c4=1, c5=1, c6=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 59:** `A²*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*cos(c4*log(A²*c5 + A*c6 + 1))`
cos(log(...)) ≠ sin(log(...)). But cos(x) = sin(x + π/2). However, the argument is log(A²*c5 + A*c6 + 1). Can we set c5=0, c6=1? Then cos(c4*log(A+1)). With c4=1, this is cos(log(A+1)) = sin(log(A+1) + π/2). But we can't add a phase shift inside. **NO MATCH** (no phase parameter)

**Candidate 61:** `A*c0/(A+c1) + A^c2*c3 + c4 + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7+1) + c8)`
Set c0=0 (kills first term), c2=2, c4=0, c6=1, c7=1, c8=0. Gives c3*A² + c5*sin(log(A+1)). **MATCH**

**Candidate 73:** `A²*c0 + c1 + c2*exp(c3/(A+c4)) + c5*sin(c6*log(A*c7+1) + c8)`
Set c2=0, c1=0, c6=1, c7=1, c8=0. **MATCH**

**Candidate 92:** `c0 + c1*log(A^c2*c3+1) + c4*sin(c5*log(A*c6+1)+c7)`
Set c1=0, c0=0 won't give A². **NO MATCH** (no A² term)

**Candidate 98:** `A²*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(A²*c4) + c5*sin(A^c6*c7 + c8)`
sin(A^c6*c7) ≠ sin(log(A+1)). **NO MATCH**
